 According to the rules relating to the conditions of service of Election Commissioners, the salary of the three Commissioners, including the Chief Election Commissioner, is equal to the salary of the Judge of the Supreme Court
 ayog ke ek varisht adhikari ke mutabik supreme court or hai court ke nyaayadhishon ke vetan main badhotaree kaa faisla 25 janvari ko adhishuchet hone ke baad chunaav ayog par bhi yah adhisuchana swat: lagu ho gai he
 With this, the three Election Commissioners, entitled to equal pay to the Supreme Court Judge and Chief Justice of the High Court, will now get a salary of Rs 2
5 lakh instead of 90 thousand
 vetan badhotaree kaa faisla ek janvari 2016 se lagu mana jayega
 As per Section 3 of the Election Commission (terms and Conditions of Service of Election Commissioners) Act 1991, the salary of the Chief Election Commissioner (and other Election Commissioners) shall be equal to the salary of the Judge of the Supreme Court
 ucchtam nyaayalay or ucch nyaayalay ke nyaayadhishon ke vetan kaa nirdhaaran ucch nyaayalay evam ucchtam nyaayalay nyaayadhish (vetan evam sevashrtein) adhinium ke madhyam se hota he

5 lakh
 jajon ko 1 janvari 2016 se badi hui selary di jaaegi

 yahaan ke sarkari hiskool main vasudev panchal (53) kii khaas pahchaan he

 vasudev prayek din pehle pani laate hai, phir puure skool main jhaadu lagaate hai, kamaron or baraamde ke farsh par poncha maarthe hai or uske baad kakshaon main jaakar bacchon ko sanskrit padhaate hai
 Sanskrit teacher has not been admitted in Girota government school for the last 23 years
 darasal, mukhyalay se kaaphi dur hone ke kaaran koi bhi shikshak yahaan aana hi nahin chahta

 The list of these 10 most popular dishes in the world tops the list of Chinese imperial dishes 'peking Duck'
 patr ke mutabik ise sarvshereshth chini vyanjan ke samakaksh mana jaataa he
 It is said about this delicious dish made from the finest spices that every person must taste it once in their life
 is batakh ke saath khaas khubi he ki ise janm ke 65 dinon baad pakaane ke liye kaata jaataa he
